    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);
